[PROMPT]:
Du bist ein erfahrener Java-Reviewer.
    Architektur: 4-Layer (Eric Evans).
    Aufgabe: Finde folgende Smells: Duplication: duplizierte Codestücke die mehrmals vorkommen und eingespart werden könnten. Gib hierbei sowohl die duplizierte als auch die originale Zeile an. Bei längeren kopierten Abschnitten gib auch hier die Zeilen als Bereich an.  negative conditionals: Es handelt sich hierbei um negativ oder doppelt negativ formulierte Bedingungen und Variablen. Einfach formulierte Negierungen in if-Anweisungen sind okay solange sie verständlich sind.  dead code: Nicht genutzer Code. Klassen, Methoden und Variablen die nie aufgerufen werden.  layer violation: Es wurde sich nicht an die Package und Ebenenstruktur gehalten. Zum Beispiel Zugriff auf den Domainlayer eines anderen Pakets. missplaced resonsibility: Dieser Code ist an der falschen Stelle. Entweder gehört er in ein anderes Package oder in einen andere Schicht oder in eine andere Klasse. Shared persistency: Zugriff auf die Repositories der Domainschicht eines anderen Packages. Anemic Entity: Domain Entities in der Domainschicht die nur über Getter oder Setter verfügen aber sonst keine Funktionen. Ausgenommen sind Repositories. Für diesen Smell brauchst du keinen Zeilenangabe, da er für die gesamte Klasse gilt. Schreib einfach nur einmal -Anemic Entity- sonst zu der enstrechenden Datei.
    Regeln:
    1. Begründe kurz jeden Fund.
    4. Gruppiere nach Datei (mit Pfad). 
    2. Format unter der Datei je Smell: [Dateiname (ohne Pfad)] [Zeile(n) X]: [Smell] [Nur bei Duplizierung: die original Zeile(n)] : [Begründung].
    3. Keine Code-Wiederholung, nur Referenzen.
    5. Wenn fertig, schreibe "ENDE".

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import jakarta.persistence.Embeddable;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailType;

@Embeddable
@EqualsAndHashCode
@Getter
@NoArgsConstructor
public class Email implements EmailType {

    @JsonProperty("emailString")
    private String email;

    public Email(String email) {
        validateEmail(email);
        this.email = email;
    }

    private void validateEmail(String email) {
        validateNotNull(email);
        validateNoSpaces(email);

        String[] parts = getEmailParts(email);
        if (parts.length != 2) {
            throw new ShopException("Email must contain exactly one '@'");
        }

        String identifier = parts[0];
        String domain = parts[1];

        if (!isValidIdentifier(identifier)) {
            throw new ShopException("Invalid email identifier part");
        }

        if (!isValidDomain(domain)) {
            throw new ShopException("Invalid email domain part");
        }
    }

    private void validateNoSpaces(String email) {
        if (!email.equals(email.trim())) {
            throw new ShopException("Email must not have leading or trailing spaces");
        }
    }

    private static void validateTLD(String domain) {
        if (!(domain.endsWith(".de") || domain.endsWith(".at") || domain.endsWith(".ch") ||
                domain.endsWith(".com") || domain.endsWith(".org"))) {
            throw new ShopException("Email must end with a valid domain (.de, .at, .ch, .com, .org)");
        }
    }

    private static void validateNotNull(String email) {
        if (email == null || email.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Email cannot be null");
        }
    }

    private static String[] getEmailParts(String email) {
        return email.split("@", -1);
    }

    private boolean isValidIdentifier(String identifier) {
        if (identifier.isEmpty()) return false;
        if (identifier.contains(" ")) return false;
        if (identifier.contains("..")) return false;
        if (!identifier.matches("[A-Za-z0-9]+(\\.[A-Za-z0-9]+)*")) return false;

        return true;
    }

    private boolean isValidDomain(String domain) {
        if (domain.isEmpty()) return false;
        if (domain.contains(" ")) return false;
        if (domain.contains("..")) return false;
        if (!domain.matches("[A-Za-z0-9]+(\\.[A-Za-z0-9]+)*")) return false;
        validateTLD(domain);
        return true;
    }

    public String getIdentifier() {
        return email.split("@", -1)[0];
    }

    public String getDomain() {
        return email.split("@", -1)[1];
    }



    public static EmailType of( String emailAsString ) {
        return new Email( emailAsString );
    }

    /**
     * A special kind of "copy constructor": Returns a new email object with
     * the same identifyer (the substring left of the "@" sign) as the current one, but
     * with a new domain substring (right of the "@" sign).
     * @param domainString - the new domain for the copied email
     * @return the new email
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *     - domainString is null
     *     - the new email would not be valid (see `of(...)` method)
     */
    @Override
    public EmailType sameIdentifyerDifferentDomain(String domainString) {
        validateNotNull(domainString);

        String identifier = getIdentifier();
        String newEmail = identifier + "@" + domainString;

        return new Email(newEmail);
        
    }

    /**
     * Another special kind of "copy constructor": Returns a new email object
     * with the same domain (the substring right of the "@" sign) as the current one, but
     * with a new identifyer substring (left of the "@" sign).
     * @param identifyerString - the new identifyer for the copied email
     * @return the new email
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *     - identifyerString is null
     *     - the new email would not be valid (see `of(...)` method)
     */
    @Override
    public EmailType sameDomainDifferentIdentifyer(String identifyerString) {
        validateNotNull(identifyerString);

        String domain = getDomain();
        String newEmail = identifyerString + "@" + domain;

        return new Email(newEmail);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return email;
    }
}

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\ST2M4_group_2767082b-b468-438e-b617-5205499d6937\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\domainprimitives\Money.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import jakarta.persistence.Embeddable;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.MoneyType;

@Embeddable
@EqualsAndHashCode
@Getter
@NoArgsConstructor
public class Money implements MoneyType {

    private Float amount;

    @JsonProperty("currency")
    private String currencyUnit;

    public Money(Float amount, String currencyUnit) {
        validateAmount(amount);
        validateCurrencyUnit(currencyUnit);

        this.amount = amount;
        this.currencyUnit = currencyUnit;
    }

    private static void validateCurrencyUnit(String currencyUnit) {
        if (currencyUnit == null || currencyUnit.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Currency unit cannot be null or empty");
        }
        if (!currencyUnit.equals("EUR") && !currencyUnit.equals("CHF")) {
            throw new ShopException("Currency unit must be 'EUR' or 'CHF'");
        }
    }

    private static void validateAmount(Float amount) {
        if (amount == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Amount cannot be null");
        }
        if (amount < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Amount cannot be negative");
        }
    }


    @Override
    public Float getAmount() {
        return amount;
    }

    @Override
    public String getCurrencyUnit() {
        return currencyUnit;
    }

    /**
     * @param otherMoney
     * @return this + otherMoney, as a new object
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - otherMoney is null
     *      - otherMoney.currencyUnit != this.currencyUnit
     */
    @Override
    public MoneyType add(MoneyType otherMoney) {
        validateMoneyNotNull(otherMoney);
        checkSameCurrencyUnit(otherMoney);

        return new Money(this.amount + otherMoney.getAmount(), this.currencyUnit);
    }

    private static void validateMoneyNotNull(MoneyType otherMoney) {
        if (otherMoney == null) {
            throw new ShopException("otherMoney cannot be null");
        }
    }

    private void checkSameCurrencyUnit(MoneyType otherMoney) {
        if (!this.currencyUnit.equals(otherMoney.getCurrencyUnit())) {
            throw new ShopException("Currency units do not match");
        }
    }

    /**
     * @param otherMoney
     * @return this - otherMoney, as a new object
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - otherMoney is null
     *      - otherMoney.currencyUnit != this.currencyUnit
     *      - otherMoney > this
     */
    @Override
    public MoneyType subtract(MoneyType otherMoney) {
        validateMoneyNotNull(otherMoney);
        checkSameCurrencyUnit(otherMoney);

        if (this.amount < otherMoney.getAmount()) {
            throw new ShopException("Cannot subtract a larger amount from a smaller one");
        }

        return new Money(this.amount - otherMoney.getAmount(), this.currencyUnit);
    }

    /**
     * @param factor
     * @return this * factor, as a new object
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *     - factor < 0
     */
    @Override
    public MoneyType multiplyBy(int factor) {
        if (factor < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Factor cannot be negative");
        }

        return new Money(this.amount * factor, this.currencyUnit);
    }

    /**
     * @param otherMoney
     * @return true, if this > otherMoney
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - otherMoney is null
     *      - otherMoney.currencyUnit != this.currencyUnit
     */
    @Override
    public boolean largerThan(MoneyType otherMoney) {
        validateMoneyNotNull(otherMoney);
        checkSameCurrencyUnit(otherMoney);

        return this.amount > otherMoney.getAmount();
    }
    /**
     * Unfortunately, Java interfaces cannot contain static methods. However, we expect the
     * implementing class to provide a static factory method (simply named "of(...)"),
     * which creates a money object from an amount and a currency unit (as string).
     * We specify this factory method here as a comment, using the Javadoc documentation style.
     *
     * @param amount the amount of money (must be >= 0)
     * @param currencyUnit the currency unit of the money (allowed values: "EUR", "CHF")
     * @return a new Money object with the given amount and currency unit
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *   - amount is null
     *   - amount < 0
     *   - currency unit is null
     *   - currency unit is not one of the allowed values
     */
    public static MoneyType of( Float amount, String currencyUnit ){
        validateAmount(amount);
        validateCurrencyUnit(currencyUnit);

        return new Money(amount, currencyUnit);
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return amount + " " + currencyUnit;
    }

}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import jakarta.persistence.Access;
import jakarta.persistence.AccessType;
import jakarta.persistence.Embeddable;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PhysicalAddressType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.ZipCodeType;

@Embeddable
@EqualsAndHashCode
@Getter
@NoArgsConstructor
@Access(AccessType.FIELD)
public class PhysicalAddress implements PhysicalAddressType {

    private String street;
    private String city;
    private ZipCode zipCode;

    public PhysicalAddress(String street, String city, ZipCode zipCode) {
        validateStreet(street);
        validateCity(city);
        validateZipCode(zipCode);

        this.street = street;
        this.city = city;
        this.zipCode = zipCode;
    }

    private void validateZipCode(ZipCodeType zipCode) {
        if (zipCode == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Zip code must not be null");
        }
    }
    private void validateCity(String city) {
        if (city == null || city.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("City must not be null or empty");
        }
    }

    private void validateStreet(String street) {
        if (street == null || street.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Street must not be null or empty");
        }
    }

    @Override
    public String getStreet() {
        return street;
    }

    @Override
    public String getCity() {
        return city;
    }

    @Override
    public ZipCodeType getZipCode() {
        return zipCode;
    }

    public static PhysicalAddressType of( String street, String city, ZipCodeType zipCode ){
        if (!(zipCode instanceof ZipCode zipCodeImpl)) {
            throw new ShopException("Only ZipCode instances are supported");
        }

        return new PhysicalAddress(street, city, zipCodeImpl);
    }
}


--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\ST2M4_group_2767082b-b468-438e-b617-5205499d6937\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\domainprimitives\ZipCode.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import jakarta.persistence.Embeddable;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.ZipCodeType;

@Embeddable
@EqualsAndHashCode
@Getter
@NoArgsConstructor
public class ZipCode implements ZipCodeType {

    @JsonProperty("zipCodeString")
    private String zipCode;

    public ZipCode(String zipCode) {
        validateZipCodeNotNull(zipCode);
        validateZipCodeFormat(zipCode);
        this.zipCode = zipCode;
    }


    /**
     * You will need some idea of "imprecise difference" between two zip codes for properly
     * implementing storage units in your shopping platform. This method calculates such a
     * difference. You can decide for yourself what values you return, unless you comply
     * with the following rules.
     * - The return value is 0 if both zip codes are the same
     * - If not:
     *      - The difference is > 0 if both zip codes differ in the last digit, like 5673x
     *        and 5673y (with x != y). However, the exact numbers for x and y don't matter.
     *        So, 56733 and 56734 have the same difference as 56733 and 56739.
     *      - The difference grows if more digits (counted from the right side) differ.
     *        So, 5abcd and 5rstu have a larger difference than 53bcd and 53stu (if abcd
     *        and rstu are not the same). Again, the precise numbers don't matter. Therefore,
     *        53876 and 54876 have the same difference as 53876 and 57261.
     *      - However, the difference between 5abcd and 6rstu must be smaller than the one
     *        between 5abcd and 7rstu, and this difference in turn must be smaller than the
     *        one between 5abcd and 9rstu.
     *      - This last condition reflects the fact the first digits of a zip code marks a region
     *        that is (usually) next to the region for an adjacent number. I.e. the "4" region
     *        is next to the "5" number. Same applies to "0" and "9", they are also next to each
     *        other.
     * @param otherZipCode
     * @return the calculated difference
     * @throws ShopException if otherZipCode is null
     */
    @Override
    public int difference(ZipCodeType otherZipCode) {
        if (otherZipCode == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Other zip code must not be null");
        }

        String other = otherZipCode.toString();

        if (this.zipCode.equals(other)) {
            return 0;
        }

        // Abweichung in den Stellen 1–4 (Ziffern 2. bis 5.)
        int diffLevel = 0;
        for (int i = 1; i < 5; i++) {
            if (this.zipCode.charAt(i) != other.charAt(i)) {
                diffLevel = 5 - i;
                break;
            }
        }

        int thisRegion = Character.getNumericValue(this.zipCode.charAt(0));
        int otherRegion = Character.getNumericValue(other.charAt(0));
        int regionDiff = regionDistance(thisRegion, otherRegion);

        return diffLevel + regionDiff * 10;
    }

    private int regionDistance(int a, int b) {
        int diff = Math.abs(a - b);
        return Math.min(diff, 10 - diff); // zyklisch: 0 und 9 sind benachbart
    }



    /**
     * For the currently used way of deciding on the best fitting storage unit for a purchase,
     * we need to know the first digit of the zip code.
     */
    @Override
    public Integer getFirstDigitZipCode() {
        String zipCodeString = this.toString();
        return Integer.parseInt(zipCodeString.substring(0, 1));
    }

    /**
     * Unfortunately, Java interfaces cannot contain static methods. However, we expect the
     * implementing class to provide a static factory method (simply named "of(...)"),
     * which creates an zip code, given as a string.
     * We specify this factory method here as a comment, using the Javadoc documentation style.
     *
     * @param zipCodeAsString - the zip code as a string.
     *      We will use a much simplified validation method to check if the zip code is valid:
     *      - It must contain exactly 5 digits.
     *      - The last 4 digits must not be 0000 (i.e. 20000 is not a valid zip code, but 20001 is valid)
     * @return a new zip code object matching the given string
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - zipCodeAsString is null
     *      - zipCodeAsString is not a valid zip code (see above)
     */
    public static ZipCodeType of( String zipCodeAsString ){
        validateZipCodeNotNull(zipCodeAsString);
        validateZipCodeFormat(zipCodeAsString);
        return new ZipCode(zipCodeAsString);
    }

    private static void validateZipCodeFormat(String zipCodeAsString) {
        if (!zipCodeAsString.matches("\\d{5}")) {
            throw new ShopException("Zip code must contain exactly 5 digits");
        }
        if (zipCodeAsString.substring(1, 5).equals("0000")) {
            throw new ShopException("Zip code cannot end with 0000");
        }
    }

    private static void validateZipCodeNotNull(String zipCodeAsString) {
        if (zipCodeAsString == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Zip code cannot be null");
        }
    }

    @Override
    public String toString() {
        return zipCode;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce;

import jakarta.persistence.Column;
import jakarta.persistence.MappedSuperclass;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.ToString;

import java.io.Serializable;
import java.util.UUID;

@MappedSuperclass
@Getter
@EqualsAndHashCode(of = "id")
@ToString(of = "id")
public abstract class GenericId implements Serializable {
    @Column(nullable = false, updatable = false)
    private final UUID id;

    protected GenericId() {
        this( UUID.randomUUID() );
    }

    protected GenericId( UUID id ) {
        this.id = id;
    }
}


--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\ST2M4_group_2767082b-b468-438e-b617-5205499d6937\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\GenericIdConverter.java ---
/*
 * Copyright ArchiLab 2025, Prof. Bente & Team, CIDE Institute, TH Köln
 */
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce;

import jakarta.persistence.AttributeConverter;
import jakarta.persistence.Converter;

import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.function.Function;


@Converter
public abstract class GenericIdConverter<T extends GenericId> implements AttributeConverter<T, UUID> {
    private final Function<UUID, T> factory;

    protected GenericIdConverter( Function<UUID, T> factory ) {
        this.factory = factory;
    }

    @Override
    public UUID convertToDatabaseColumn( T attribute ) {
        return attribute == null ? null : attribute.getId();
    }

    @Override
    public T convertToEntityAttribute( UUID dbData ) {
        return dbData == null ? null : factory.apply( dbData );
    }
}

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\ST2M4_group_2767082b-b468-438e-b617-5205499d6937\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\product\application\applicationServices\ProductCatalogService.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application.applicationServices;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Money;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.entities.Product;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.repositories.ProductRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ProductCatalogUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.MoneyType;

import java.util.UUID;


@Service
public class ProductCatalogService implements ProductCatalogUseCases {
    private final ProductRepository productRepository;
    private final PurchaseProductUsageChecker purchaseChecker;
    private final ShoppingCartProductUsageChecker cartChecker;
    private final StorageUnitProductUsageChecker stockChecker;
    @Autowired
    public ProductCatalogService(ProductRepository productRepository,
                                 PurchaseProductUsageChecker purchaseChecker,
                                 ShoppingCartProductUsageChecker cartChecker,
                                 StorageUnitProductUsageChecker stockChecker) {
        this.productRepository = productRepository;
        this.purchaseChecker = purchaseChecker;
        this.cartChecker = cartChecker;
        this.stockChecker = stockChecker;
    }

    /**
     * Adds a new product to the shop catalog
     * @param name
     * @param descriptionOf
     * @param size
     * @param buyingPrice
     * @param salesPrice
     * @return the id of the new product
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *         - the product id already exists,
     *         - name or description are null or empty,
     *         - the size is <= 0 (but can be null!),
     *         - the buying price is null or <= 0,
     *         - the sales price is null or <= 0,
     *         - the sales price is lower than the buying price
     */
    @Override
    public UUID addProductToCatalog(String name, String descriptionOf, Float size, MoneyType buyingPrice, MoneyType salesPrice) {

        if (buyingPrice == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Buying price must not be null");
        }
        if (salesPrice == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Sales price must not be null");
        }
        if (name == null || name.isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Name must not be null or empty");
        }
        if (descriptionOf == null || descriptionOf.isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Description must not be null or empty");
        }
        if (size != null && size <= 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Size must be greater than 0, or null");
        }
        if (buyingPrice.largerThan(salesPrice)) {
            throw new ShopException("Sales price must not be larger than buying price");
        }

        Product product = new Product(
                name,
                descriptionOf,
                size != null ? size.doubleValue() : null,
                (Money) buyingPrice,
                (Money) salesPrice
        );

        ensureProductIdDoesNotExist(product.getId().getId());
        productRepository.save(product);
        return product.getId().getId();
    }

    /**
     * Removes a product from the shop catalog
     * @param productId
     * @throws ShopException if
     *      - the product id does not exist
     *      - the product is still in stock
     *      - the product is still in a shopping cart, or referenced by a completed purchase
     */
    @Override
    public void removeProductFromCatalog(UUID productId) {
        ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);
        ensureProductNotInStock(productId);
        ensureProductNotInShoppingCart(productId);
        ensureProductNotInPurchase(productId);

        productRepository.deleteById(new ProductId(productId));
    }

    /**
     * Get the sales price of a given product
     * @param productId
     * @return the sales price
     * @throws ShopException if the product id does not exist
     */
    @Override
    public MoneyType getSalesPrice(UUID productId) {
        return getExistingProductOrThrow(productId).getSellingPrice();
    }

    /**
     * Clears the product catalog, i.e. removes all products from the catalog, including all the stock,
     * all the reservations and all the purchases.
     */
    @Override
    public void deleteProductCatalog() {
        productRepository.deleteAll();
    }

    private void ensureProductIdDoesNotExist(UUID id) {
        if (productRepository.existsById(new ProductId(id))) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID already exists");
        }
    }

    public void ensureProductIdDoesExist(UUID productId) {
        if (!productRepository.existsById(new ProductId(productId))) {
            throw new ShopException("Product ID does not exist");
        }
    }

    public Product getExistingProductOrThrow(UUID productId) {
        return productRepository.findById(new ProductId(productId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Product with this ID does not exist"));
    }

    public void ensureProductNotInPurchase(UUID productId) {
        if (purchaseChecker.isProductInPurchase(productId)) {
            throw new ShopException("Product is already in a purchase");
        }
    }

    public void ensureProductNotInShoppingCart(UUID productId) {
        if (cartChecker.isProductInShoppingCart(productId)) {
            throw new ShopException("Product is already in a shopping cart");
        }
    }

    public void ensureProductNotInStock(UUID productId) {
        if (stockChecker.isProductInStock(productId)) {
            throw new ShopException("Product is in stock");
        }
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.entities;

import jakarta.persistence.EmbeddedId;
import jakarta.persistence.Entity;
import lombok.*;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Money;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.MoneyType;


@Entity
@Getter
@Setter
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class Product {
    @Setter(AccessLevel.PRIVATE)    // only for JPA
    @EmbeddedId
    private ProductId id;

    private String name;
    private String description;
    private Double size;
    private Money buyingPrice;
    private Money sellingPrice;

    public Product(String name, String descriptionOf, Double size, Money buyingPrice, Money salesPrice) {

        validateName(name);
        validateDescription(descriptionOf);
        validateSize(size);

        this.id = new ProductId();
        this.name = name;
        this.description = descriptionOf;
        this.size = size;
        this.buyingPrice = buyingPrice;
        this.sellingPrice = salesPrice;
    }


    private void validateName(String name) {
        if (name == null || name.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Name must not be null or empty");
        }
    }

    private void validateDescription(String description) {
        if (description == null || description.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Description must not be null or empty");
        }
    }

    private void validateSize(Double size) {
        if (size != null && size <= 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Size must be greater than 0");
        }
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.application.applicationServices;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application.applicationServices.PurchaseProductUsageChecker;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.entities.Purchase;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.repositories.PurchaseRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.valueObjects.PurchasePart;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class PurchaseCheckerService implements PurchaseProductUsageChecker {

    private final PurchaseRepository purchaseRepository;

    @Autowired
    public PurchaseCheckerService(PurchaseRepository purchaseRepository) {
        this.purchaseRepository = purchaseRepository;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isProductInPurchase(UUID productId) {
        List<Purchase> purchases = (List<Purchase>) purchaseRepository.findAll();
        for (Purchase purchase : purchases) {
            for (PurchasePart part : purchase.getPurchaseParts()) {
                if (part.getProduct().getId().equals(new ProductId(productId))) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.application.applicationServices;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Email;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.entities.Purchase;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.repositories.PurchaseRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.valueObjects.PurchaseId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.valueObjects.PurchasePart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.application.applicationServices.UserRegistrationService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.entities.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.PurchaseUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailType;

import java.util.*;


@Service
public class PurchaseService implements PurchaseUseCases {
    private final PurchaseRepository purchaseRepository;
    private final UserRegistrationService userRegistrationService;
    @Autowired
    public PurchaseService( PurchaseRepository purchaseRepository, UserRegistrationService userRegistrationService) {
        this.purchaseRepository = purchaseRepository;
        this.userRegistrationService = userRegistrationService;
    }


    /**
     * Returns a map showing which products have been purchased by a user and how many of each product
     *
     * @param userEmail
     * @return the purchase history of the user (map is empty if the user has not purchased anything yet)
     * @throws ShopException if
     *      - userEmail is null or empty
     *      - the user with the given email does not exist
     */
    @Override
    public Map<UUID, Integer> getPurchaseHistory(EmailType userEmail) {

        Map<UUID, Integer> purchaseHistory = new HashMap<>();

        User user = userRegistrationService.getExistingUserOrThrow((Email) userEmail);

        purchaseRepository.findAll().forEach(purchase -> {
            if (purchase.getUser().getId().equals(user.getId())) {
                purchase.getPurchaseParts().forEach(
                        purchasePart -> {
                            UUID productId = purchasePart.getProduct().getId().getId();
                            int quantity = purchasePart.getQuantity();
                            purchaseHistory.put(productId, purchaseHistory.getOrDefault(productId, 0) + quantity);
                        }
                );
            }
        });

        return purchaseHistory;
    }


    /**
     * @return the number of products in a given purchase. If the product is not a part of the purchase, the method
     *         returns 0. No exception is thrown.
     * @param purchaseId - the id of the purchase to be checked
     * @param productId - the id of the product for which we want to know the quantity
     * @throws ShopException if
     *     - purchaseId is null, or doesn't exist in the system
     *     - productId is null, or doesn't exist in the system
     */
    @Override
    public Integer getPurchaseQuantityOfProduct(UUID purchaseId, UUID productId) {

        PurchaseId purchaseId1 = new PurchaseId(purchaseId);
        Purchase purchase = purchaseRepository.findById(purchaseId1)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Purchase with ID " + purchaseId + " does not exist."));

        List<PurchasePart> parts = purchase.getPurchaseParts();
        for (PurchasePart part : parts) {
            if (part.getProduct().getId().getId().equals(productId)) {
                return part.getQuantity();
            }
        }

        return 0;
    }



    /**
     * @return the id of the storage unit that is responsible for the given purchase
     * @param purchaseId - the id of the purchase to be checked
     * @throws ShopException if
     *      - purchaseId is null, or doesn't exist in the system
     */
    @Override
    public UUID getStorageUnitIdForPurchase(UUID purchaseId) {

        PurchaseId purchaseId1 = new PurchaseId(purchaseId);
        Purchase purchase = purchaseRepository.findById(purchaseId1)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Purchase with ID " + purchaseId + " does not exist."));

        return purchase.getStorageUnit().getId().getId();
    }

    @Override
    public void deleteAllPurchases() {
        purchaseRepository.deleteAll();
    }

    public Purchase getPurchaseById(UUID purchaseId) {
        PurchaseId id = new PurchaseId(purchaseId);
        return purchaseRepository.findById(id)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Purchase with ID " + purchaseId + " does not exist."));
    }


}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application.applicationServices;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application.applicationServices.ShoppingCartProductUsageChecker;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.entities.ShoppingCart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.repositories.ShoppingCartRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.valueObjects.ShoppingCartPart;

import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class ShoppingCartCheckerService implements ShoppingCartProductUsageChecker {

    private final ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository;

    @Autowired
    public ShoppingCartCheckerService(ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository) {
        this.shoppingCartRepository = shoppingCartRepository;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isProductInShoppingCart(UUID productId) {
        List<ShoppingCart> carts = (List<ShoppingCart>) shoppingCartRepository.findAll();
        for (ShoppingCart cart : carts) {
            for (ShoppingCartPart part : cart.getShoppingCartParts()) {
                if (part.getProduct().getId().equals(new ProductId(productId))) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }

--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\ST2M4_group_2767082b-b468-438e-b617-5205499d6937\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\shoppingcart\application\ShoppingCartController.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
import org.springframework.http.ResponseEntity;
import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.*;
import org.springframework.web.method.annotation.MethodArgumentTypeMismatchException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.InsufficientStockException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Email;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmptyCartException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Money;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.application.applicationServices.PurchaseService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.entities.Purchase;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.valueObjects.PurchasePart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.entities.ShoppingCart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.application.applicationServices.UserRegistrationService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;

import java.net.URI;
import java.util.*;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;

@RestController
public class ShoppingCartController {
    private final ShoppingCartService shoppingCartService;
    private final PurchaseService purchaseService;

    @Autowired
    public ShoppingCartController(ShoppingCartService shoppingCartService, PurchaseService purchaseService) {
        this.shoppingCartService = shoppingCartService;
        this.purchaseService = purchaseService;

    }

    @GetMapping(value = "/shoppingCarts", params = "userId", produces = "application/json")
    public ResponseEntity<ShoppingCartDTO> getCartForUser(@RequestParam UUID userId) {

        ShoppingCart cart;
        try {
            cart = shoppingCartService.getCartByUserId(userId);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build(); // Not Found if the user does not exist
        }

        if (cart == null) {
            cart = shoppingCartService.createCartIfNotExists(userId);
        }
        ShoppingCartDTO dto = mapToDTO(cart);
        return ResponseEntity.ok(dto);
    }

    @GetMapping(value = "/shoppingCarts", produces = "application/json")
    public ResponseEntity<Void> handleMissingUserIdParam() {
        return ResponseEntity.status(405).build(); // Method Not Allowed
    }

    private ShoppingCartDTO mapToDTO(ShoppingCart cart) {
        List<ShoppingCartPartDTO> partDTOs = cart.getShoppingCartParts().stream()
                .map(part -> new ShoppingCartPartDTO(part.getProduct().getId().getId(), part.getQuantity()))
                .collect(Collectors.toList());

        String formattedPrice = formatPrice( (Money) shoppingCartService.getShoppingCartAsMoneyValue( (Email) cart.getUser().getEmail()));

        return new ShoppingCartDTO(cart.getId().getId(), formattedPrice, partDTOs);
    }

    private String formatPrice(Money money) {
        Float amount = money.getAmount(); // z. B. 21.34
        String currency = money.getCurrencyUnit(); // z. B. "EUR"

        String symbol = switch (currency) {
            case "EUR" -> "€";
            case "CHF" -> "CHF";
            default -> currency;
        };

        return String.format(Locale.getDefault(), "%.2f %s", amount, symbol);
    }

    @PostMapping("/shoppingCarts/{shoppingCartId}/parts")
    public ResponseEntity<Void> addPartToCart(
            @PathVariable UUID shoppingCartId,
            @RequestBody ShoppingCartPartDTO partDTO
            ) {
        if(partDTO.getProductId() == null || partDTO.getQuantity() <= 0) {
            return ResponseEntity.unprocessableEntity().build(); // Bad Request if productId is null or quantity is invalid
        }
        try {
            UserType user = shoppingCartService.getUserByShoppingCartId(shoppingCartId);
            shoppingCartService.addProductToShoppingCart(user.getEmail(), partDTO.getProductId(), partDTO.getQuantity());
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build(); // Not Found if the shopping cart or product does not exist
        }
            return new ResponseEntity<>(HttpStatus.CREATED);
    }

    @ExceptionHandler(MethodArgumentTypeMismatchException.class)
    public ResponseEntity<Void> handleInvalidUUID(MethodArgumentTypeMismatchException ex) {
        if ("userId".equals(ex.getName()) && ex.getRequiredType() == UUID.class) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND).build();
        }
        return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST).build();
    }

    @DeleteMapping("/shoppingCarts/{shoppingCartId}/parts/{productId}")
    public ResponseEntity<Void> removeProductFromCart(
            @PathVariable UUID shoppingCartId,
            @PathVariable UUID productId
    ) {
        try {
            UserType user = shoppingCartService.getUserByShoppingCartId(shoppingCartId);
            shoppingCartService.removeProductFromShoppingCart(user.getEmail(), productId);
            return ResponseEntity.ok().build(); // 204: Erfolgreich gelöscht, keine Rückgabe
        } catch (ShopException e) {
            return ResponseEntity.notFound().build(); // z. B. wenn cart oder Produkt nicht existiert
        }
    }

    @PostMapping("/shoppingCarts/{shoppingCartId}/checkout")
    public ResponseEntity<List<Map<String, Object>>> checkoutCart(@PathVariable UUID shoppingCartId) {
        try {
            UserType user = shoppingCartService.getUserByShoppingCartId(shoppingCartId);
            Set<UUID> purchaseIds = shoppingCartService.checkout(user.getEmail());

            List<Map<String, Object>> responseList = new ArrayList<>();
            for (UUID purchaseId : purchaseIds) {
                Purchase purchase = purchaseService.getPurchaseById(purchaseId);

                Map<String, Object> purchaseMap = new LinkedHashMap<>();
                purchaseMap.put("id", purchase.getId().getId());
                purchaseMap.put("userName", purchase.getUser().getName());
                purchaseMap.put("storageUnitId", purchase.getStorageUnit().getId().getId());

                List<Map<String, Object>> partsList = new ArrayList<>();
                for (PurchasePart part : purchase.getPurchaseParts()) {
                    Map<String, Object> partMap = new LinkedHashMap<>();
                    partMap.put("productId", part.getProduct().getId().getId());
                    partMap.put("quantity", part.getQuantity());
                    partsList.add(partMap);
                }

                purchaseMap.put("parts", partsList);
                responseList.add(purchaseMap);
            }

            return ResponseEntity.created(URI.create("/purchases")).body(responseList); // 201: Created with body
        } catch (EmptyCartException e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CONFLICT).build();
        } catch (InsufficientStockException e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CONFLICT).build(); // <-- 409 für Lagerkonflikte
        } catch (ShopException e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.CONFLICT).build(); // z. B. leerer Warenkorb o. Ä.
        }
    }


}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.application;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.InsufficientStockException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Email;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.EmptyCartException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.Money;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.ZipCode;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application.applicationServices.ProductCatalogService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.entities.Product;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.entities.Purchase;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.repositories.PurchaseRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.purchase.domain.valueObjects.PurchasePart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.entities.ShoppingCart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.repositories.ShoppingCartRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.valueObjects.ShoppingCartId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.valueObjects.ShoppingCartPart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.application.applicationServices.StorageUnitService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.StorageUnit;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.StorageUnitComparator;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.application.applicationServices.UserRegistrationService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.entities.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.ShoppingCartUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.MoneyType;

import java.util.*;

@Service
public class ShoppingCartService implements ShoppingCartUseCases {

    private final ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository;
    private final UserRegistrationService userRegistrationService;
    private final ProductCatalogService productCatalogService;
    private final StorageUnitService storageUnitService;
    private final PurchaseRepository purchaseRepository;

    @Autowired
    public ShoppingCartService(ShoppingCartRepository shoppingCartRepository, UserRegistrationService userRegistrationService, ProductCatalogService productCatalogService, StorageUnitService storageUnitService, PurchaseRepository purchaseRepository) {
        this.shoppingCartRepository = shoppingCartRepository;
        this.userRegistrationService = userRegistrationService;
        this.productCatalogService = productCatalogService;
        this.storageUnitService = storageUnitService;
        this.purchaseRepository = purchaseRepository;
    }

    /**
     * Adds a product to the cart of a user
     *
     * @param userEmail
     * @param productId
     * @param quantityOf
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *                       - userEmail is null or empty,
     *                       - the user with the given email does not exist,
     *                       - productId is null,
     *                       - the product with productId does not exist
     *                       - the Quantity is negative,
     */
    @Override
    public void addProductToShoppingCart(EmailType userEmail, UUID productId, int quantityOf) {
        userRegistrationService.ensureUserExists((Email) userEmail);
        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) userEmail);
        if (shoppingCart == null) {
            User user = userRegistrationService.getExistingUserOrThrow((Email) userEmail);
            shoppingCart = new ShoppingCart(user, new ArrayList<>());
        }

        List<ShoppingCartPart> parts = shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts();
        List<ShoppingCartPart> updatedParts = new ArrayList<>();

        boolean productFound = false;

        for (ShoppingCartPart part : parts) {
            if (part.getProduct().getId().equals(new ProductId(productId))) {
                updatedParts.add(new ShoppingCartPart(part.getProduct(), part.getQuantity() + quantityOf));
                productFound = true;
            } else {
                updatedParts.add(part);
            }
        }

        if (!productFound) {
            updatedParts.add(new ShoppingCartPart(productCatalogService.getExistingProductOrThrow(productId), quantityOf));
        }

        shoppingCart.setShoppingCartParts(updatedParts);
        shoppingCartRepository.save(shoppingCart);
    }

    /**
     * Removes a product from the cart of a user
     *
     * @param userEmail
     * @param productId
     * @param quantityOf
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *                       - userEmail is null or empty,
     *                       - the user with the given email does not exist,
     *                       - productId is null,
     *                       - the product with productId does not exist
     *                       - the Quantity is negative
     *                       - the product is not in the shopping cart in the requested Quantity
     */
    @Override
    public void removeProductFromShoppingCart(EmailType userEmail, UUID productId, int quantityOf) {
        userRegistrationService.ensureUserExists((Email) userEmail);
        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) userEmail);
        if (shoppingCart == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Shopping cart not found for user: " + userEmail);
        }

        List<ShoppingCartPart> parts = shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts();
        List<ShoppingCartPart> updatedParts = new ArrayList<>();

        boolean productFound = false;

        for (ShoppingCartPart part : parts) {
            if (part.getProduct().getId().equals(new ProductId(productId))) {
                if (part.getQuantity() < quantityOf) {
                    throw new ShopException("Not enough quantity in shopping cart");
                }
                updatedParts.add(new ShoppingCartPart(part.getProduct(), part.getQuantity() - quantityOf));
                productFound = true;
            } else {
                updatedParts.add(part);
            }
        }

        if (!productFound) {
            throw new ShopException("Product not found in shopping cart");
        }

        shoppingCart.setShoppingCartParts(updatedParts);
        shoppingCartRepository.save(shoppingCart);
    }

    public void removeProductFromShoppingCart(EmailType userEmail, UUID productId) {
        userRegistrationService.ensureUserExists((Email) userEmail);
        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) userEmail);
        if (shoppingCart == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Shopping cart not found for user: " + userEmail);
        }

        List<ShoppingCartPart> parts = shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts();
        List<ShoppingCartPart> updatedParts = new ArrayList<>();

        boolean productFound = false;

        for (ShoppingCartPart part : parts) {
            if (part.getProduct().getId().equals(new ProductId(productId))) {
                productFound = true;
                continue;
            } else {
                updatedParts.add(part);
            }
        }

        if (!productFound) {
            throw new ShopException("Product not found in shopping cart");
        }

        shoppingCart.setShoppingCartParts(updatedParts);
        shoppingCartRepository.save(shoppingCart);
    }

    /**
     * Returns a map showing which products are in the cart of a user and how many of each product
     *
     * @param userEmail
     * @return the cart of the user (map is empty if the cart is empty)
     * @throws ShopException if
     *                       - the user with the given email does not exist
     */
    @Override
    public Map<UUID, Integer> getShoppingCartAsMap(EmailType userEmail) {
        userRegistrationService.ensureUserExists((Email) userEmail);

        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) userEmail);
        if (shoppingCart == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Shopping cart not found for user: " + userEmail);
        }
        Map<UUID, Integer> shoppingCartMap = new HashMap<>();

        for (ShoppingCartPart part : shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts()) {
            shoppingCartMap.put(part.getProduct().getId().getId(), part.getQuantity());
        }
        return shoppingCartMap;
    }

    /**
     * Returns the current value of all products in the cart of a user
     *
     * @param userEmail
     * @return the cart of the user
     * @throws ShopException if the user with the given email does not exist
     */
    @Override
    public MoneyType getShoppingCartAsMoneyValue(EmailType userEmail) {
        userRegistrationService.ensureUserExists((Email) userEmail);


        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) userEmail);
        if (shoppingCart == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Shopping cart not found for user: " + userEmail);
        }

        MoneyType totalValue = new Money((float) 0, "EUR");
        for (ShoppingCartPart part : shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts()) {
            totalValue = totalValue.add(part.getProduct().getSellingPrice().multiplyBy(part.getQuantity()));
        }
        return totalValue;
    }


    @Override
    public Set<UUID> checkout(EmailType userEmail) {
        userRegistrationService.ensureUserExists((Email) userEmail);
        User user = userRegistrationService.getExistingUserOrThrow((Email) userEmail);
        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) userEmail);
        ensureShoppingCartNotEmpty(shoppingCart);

        // 1. Erstelle Map<ProductId, Integer> aus dem Warenkorb
        Map<ProductId, Integer> remainingParts = new HashMap<>();
        for (ShoppingCartPart part : shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts()) {
            remainingParts.put(part.getProduct().getId(), part.getQuantity());
        }

        Set<UUID> purchaseIds = new HashSet<>();
        List<StorageUnit> allStorageUnits = storageUnitService.getAllStorageUnits();

        while (!remainingParts.isEmpty()) {
            // 2. Sortiere StorageUnits mit Comparator
            allStorageUnits.sort(new StorageUnitComparator(remainingParts, (ZipCode) user.getAddress().getZipCode()));
            StorageUnit bestStorageUnit = allStorageUnits.get(0);

            Set<ProductId> fulfillable = bestStorageUnit.fulfillableShoppingCartParts(remainingParts);
            if (fulfillable.isEmpty()) {
                throw new InsufficientStockException("No storage unit can fulfill remaining shopping cart parts.");
            }

            List<PurchasePart> purchaseParts = new ArrayList<>();

            for (ProductId productId : fulfillable) {
                int quantity = remainingParts.get(productId);
                storageUnitService.removeFromStock(bestStorageUnit.getId().getId(), productId.getId(), quantity);

                Product product = shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts().stream()
                        .filter(part -> part.getProduct().getId().equals(productId))
                        .findFirst()
                        .orElseThrow()
                        .getProduct();

                purchaseParts.add(new PurchasePart(quantity, product));
            }

            Purchase purchase = new Purchase(user, purchaseParts, bestStorageUnit);
            purchaseRepository.save(purchase);
            purchaseIds.add(purchase.getId().getId());

            // Entferne ausgelieferte Produkte aus der Map
            fulfillable.forEach(remainingParts::remove);
        }

        shoppingCartRepository.delete(shoppingCart);
        return purchaseIds;
    }


    @Override
    public void emptyAllShoppingCarts() {
        shoppingCartRepository.deleteAll();
    }

    private void ensureShoppingCartNotEmpty(ShoppingCart shoppingCart) {
        if (shoppingCart == null || shoppingCart.getShoppingCartParts().isEmpty()) {
            throw new EmptyCartException("Shopping cart is empty");
        }
    }

    public ShoppingCart getCartByUserId(UUID userId) {
        User user = userRegistrationService.getExistingUserByIdOrThrow(userId);
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) user.getEmail());
        if (cart == null) {
            return null;
        }
        return cart;
    }

    public User getUserByShoppingCartId(UUID shoppingCartId) {
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findById(new ShoppingCartId(shoppingCartId))
                .orElseThrow(() -> new ShopException("Shopping cart not found for ID: " + shoppingCartId));
        return cart.getUser();
    }

    public ShoppingCart getCartByUserEmail(Email email) {
        ShoppingCart cart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) email);
        if (cart == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Shopping cart not found for user: " + email);
        }
        return cart;
    }

    public ShoppingCart createCartIfNotExists(UUID userId) {
        User user = userRegistrationService.getExistingUserByIdOrThrow(userId);
        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) user.getEmail());
        if (shoppingCart != null) {
            return shoppingCart;
        }
        shoppingCart = new ShoppingCart(user, new ArrayList<>());
        shoppingCartRepository.save(shoppingCart);
        return shoppingCart;
    }
    public ShoppingCart createCartIfNotExists(EmailType email) {
        User user = userRegistrationService.getExistingUserOrThrow((Email) email);
        ShoppingCart shoppingCart = shoppingCartRepository.findByUserEmail((Email) user.getEmail());
        if (shoppingCart != null) {
            return shoppingCart;
        }
        shoppingCart = new ShoppingCart(user, new ArrayList<>());
        shoppingCartRepository.save(shoppingCart);
        return shoppingCart;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.entities;

import jakarta.persistence.*;
import lombok.*;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.valueObjects.ShoppingCartId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.valueObjects.ShoppingCartPart;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.user.domain.entities.User;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;

import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.List;

@Entity
@Setter
@Getter
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class ShoppingCart {
    @Setter(AccessLevel.PRIVATE)    // only for JPA
    @EmbeddedId
    private ShoppingCartId id;

    @OneToOne
    private User user;

    @ElementCollection(fetch = FetchType.EAGER)
    private List<ShoppingCartPart> shoppingCartParts;

    public ShoppingCart(User user, List<ShoppingCartPart> shoppingCartParts) {
        this.id = new ShoppingCartId();
        this.user = user;
        this.shoppingCartParts = shoppingCartParts;
    }

    public ShoppingCart(UserType user) {
        this.id = new ShoppingCartId();
        this.user = (User) user;
        this.shoppingCartParts = Collections.emptyList();
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.shoppingcart.domain.valueObjects;

import jakarta.persistence.Embeddable;
import jakarta.persistence.FetchType;
import jakarta.persistence.ManyToOne;
import lombok.AllArgsConstructor;
import lombok.EqualsAndHashCode;
import lombok.Getter;
import lombok.NoArgsConstructor;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.entities.Product;

@Embeddable
@EqualsAndHashCode
@Getter
@NoArgsConstructor
public class ShoppingCartPart {
    private int quantity;

    @ManyToOne(fetch = FetchType.EAGER)
    private Product product;

    public ShoppingCartPart(Product product, int quantity) {
        checkQuantityLargerThenZero(quantity);

        this.product = product;
        this.quantity = quantity;
    }

    private static void checkQuantityLargerThenZero(int quantity) {
        if (quantity < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Quantity cannot be negative");
        }
    }

}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.application.applicationServices;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application.applicationServices.StorageUnitProductUsageChecker;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.StorageUnit;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.repositories.StorageUnitRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.valueObjects.StockLevel;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class StorageUnitCheckerService implements StorageUnitProductUsageChecker {

    private final StorageUnitRepository storageUnitRepository;

    @Autowired
    public StorageUnitCheckerService(StorageUnitRepository storageUnitRepository) {
        this.storageUnitRepository = storageUnitRepository;
    }

    @Override
    public boolean isProductInStock(UUID productId) {
        List<StorageUnit> units = (List<StorageUnit>) storageUnitRepository.findAll();
        for (StorageUnit unit : units) {
            for (StockLevel level : unit.getStockLevels()) {
                if (level.getProduct().getId().equals(new ProductId(productId))) {
                    return true;
                }
            }
        }
        return false;
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.application.applicationServices;

import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.InsufficientStockException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;

import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.application.applicationServices.ProductCatalogService;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.entities.Product;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.StorageUnit;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.repositories.StorageUnitRepository;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.valueObjects.StockLevel;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.valueObjects.StorageUnitId;

import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PhysicalAddressType;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.UUID;

@Service
public class StorageUnitService implements StorageUnitUseCases {

    private final StorageUnitRepository storageUnitRepository;
    private final ProductCatalogService productCatalogService;
    @Autowired
    public StorageUnitService(StorageUnitRepository storageUnitRepository, ProductCatalogService productCatalogService) {
        this.storageUnitRepository = storageUnitRepository;
        this.productCatalogService = productCatalogService;
    }



    /**
     *
     * @param name
     * @param physicalAddress
     * @return the id of the new storage unit
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - name is null or empty
     *      - physicalAddress is null
     */

    @Override
    public UUID addNewStorageUnit(String name, PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress) {

        if (name == null || name.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Name must not be null or empty");
        }
        if (physicalAddress == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Address must not be null");
        }

        StorageUnit storageUnit = new StorageUnit(
                name,
                (PhysicalAddress) physicalAddress,
                new ArrayList<>()
        );

        storageUnitRepository.save(storageUnit);
        return storageUnit.getId().getId();
    }

    /**
     * Deletes all storage units from the shop. Intended for testing purposes.
     */
    @Override
    public void deleteAllStorageUnits() {
        storageUnitRepository.deleteAll();
    }

    /**
     * Find the suitable storage unit to serve the purchase for a user.
     * @param zipCode the zip code of the user who wants to buy
     * @return the id of the storage unit that is suitable for the purchase (or any of the fitting storage units,
     *         if there are several storage units with the same zip code range)
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *     - zipCode is null, empty, or not a valid zip code
     *     - no storage unit is available for the given zipCode
     */

    /*
    @Override
    public UUID findSuitableStorageUnit(String zipCode) {

        int firstDigit = Integer.parseInt(zipCode.substring(0, 1));
        ArrayList <StorageUnit> storageUnits = new ArrayList<>();

        storageUnitRepository.findAll().forEach(
                storageUnit -> {
                    if (storageUnit.getFromZipCodeFirstDigit() <= firstDigit
                            && storageUnit.getToZipCodeFirstDigit() >= firstDigit) {
                        storageUnits.add(storageUnit);
                    }
                }
        );

        if (storageUnits.isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("No storage unit available for the given zip code");
        }
        return storageUnits.get(0).getId().getId();
    }
*/

    /**
     * Adds a certain Quantity of a given product to the stock
     * @param storageUnitId
     * @param productId
     * @param addedQuantityOf
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - storageUnitId is null
     *      - the storage unit with that id does not exist
     *      - productId is null
     *      - the product with that id does not exist
     *      - addedQuantityOf < 0
     */
    @Override
    public void addToStock(UUID storageUnitId, UUID productId, int addedQuantityOf) {

        if(addedQuantityOf < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Added quantity must be greater than or equal to zero");
        }

        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        Product product = productCatalogService.getExistingProductOrThrow(productId);
        StorageUnit storageUnit = getExistingStorageUnitOrThrow(storageUnitId);

        List<StockLevel> stockLevels = storageUnit.getStockLevels();
        List<StockLevel> updatedStockLevels = new ArrayList<>();

        boolean productFound = false;

        for (StockLevel stockLevel : stockLevels) {
            if (stockLevel.getProduct().getId().getId().equals(productId)) {
                productFound = true;
                updatedStockLevels.add(new StockLevel(stockLevel.getQuantityOfProducts() + addedQuantityOf, product));
            } else {
                updatedStockLevels.add(stockLevel);
            }
        }

        if (!productFound) {
            updatedStockLevels.add(new StockLevel(addedQuantityOf, product));
        }

        storageUnit.setStockLevels(updatedStockLevels);
        storageUnitRepository.save(storageUnit);
    }


    /**
     * Removes a certain Quantity of a given product from the stock.
     * @param storageUnitId
     * @param productId
     * @param removedQuantityOf
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - storageUnitId is null
     *      - the storage unit with that id does not exist
     *      - productId is null
     *      - the product with that id does not exist
     *      - removedQuantityOf < 0
     */
    @Override
    public void removeFromStock(UUID storageUnitId, UUID productId, int removedQuantityOf) {

        if (removedQuantityOf == 0) {
            return;
        }

        if(removedQuantityOf < 0) {
            throw new ShopException("Added quantity must be greater than or equal to zero");
        }

        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        Product product = productCatalogService.getExistingProductOrThrow(productId);
        StorageUnit storageUnit = getExistingStorageUnitOrThrow(storageUnitId);

        List<StockLevel> stockLevels = storageUnit.getStockLevels();

        List<StockLevel> updatedStockLevels = new ArrayList<>();

        boolean productFound = false;

        for (StockLevel stockLevel : stockLevels) {
            if (stockLevel.getProduct().getId().getId().equals(productId)) {
                productFound = true;

                int updatedQuantity = stockLevel.getQuantityOfProducts() - removedQuantityOf;

                if (updatedQuantity >= 0) {
                    updatedStockLevels.add(new StockLevel(updatedQuantity, product));
                } else {
                    throw new InsufficientStockException("Not enough stock to remove the requested quantity");
                }
            } else {
                updatedStockLevels.add(stockLevel);
            }
        }

        if (!productFound) {
            throw new InsufficientStockException("Product not found in the stock.");
        }

        storageUnit.setStockLevels(updatedStockLevels);
        storageUnitRepository.save(storageUnit);
    }

    /**
     * Changes the total Quantity of a given product in the stock.
     * @param storageUnitId
     * @param productId
     * @param newTotalQuantityOf
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - storageUnitId is null
     *      - the storage unit with that id does not exist
     *      - productId is null
     *      - the product with that id does not exist
     *      - newTotalQuantityOf < 0
     */
    @Override
    public void changeStockTo(UUID storageUnitId, UUID productId, int newTotalQuantityOf) {
        ensureStorageUnitExists(storageUnitId);
        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        Product product = productCatalogService.getExistingProductOrThrow(productId);
        StorageUnit storageUnit = getExistingStorageUnitOrThrow(storageUnitId);

        List<StockLevel> stockLevels = storageUnit.getStockLevels();
        List<StockLevel> updatedStockLevels = new ArrayList<>();
        boolean productFound = false;

        for (StockLevel stockLevel : stockLevels) {
            if (stockLevel.getProduct().getId().getId().equals(productId)) {
                updatedStockLevels.add(new StockLevel(newTotalQuantityOf, product));
                productFound = true;
            } else {
                updatedStockLevels.add(stockLevel);
            }
        }

        if (!productFound) {
            updatedStockLevels.add(new StockLevel(newTotalQuantityOf, product));
        }

        storageUnit.setStockLevels(updatedStockLevels);
        storageUnitRepository.save(storageUnit);
    }

    /**
     * Get the current stock of a given product in one specific storage unit.
     * @param storageUnitId
     * @param productId
     * @return the current total stock of the product
     * @throws ShopException if ...
     *      - storageUnitId is null
     *      - the storage unit with that id does not exist
     *      - productId is null
     *      - the product with that id does not exist
     */
    @Override
    public int getAvailableStock(UUID storageUnitId, UUID productId) {
        productCatalogService.ensureProductIdDoesExist(productId);

        Product product = productCatalogService.getExistingProductOrThrow(productId);
        StorageUnit storageUnit = getExistingStorageUnitOrThrow(storageUnitId);

        for (StockLevel stockLevel : storageUnit.getStockLevels()) {
            if (stockLevel.getProduct().getId().getId().equals(product.getId().getId())) {
                return stockLevel.getQuantityOfProducts();
            }
        }
        return 0;
    }

    public StorageUnit getExistingStorageUnitOrThrow(UUID storageUnitId) {
        StorageUnit storageUnit = storageUnitRepository.findById(new StorageUnitId(storageUnitId)).orElse(null);
        if (storageUnit == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Storage unit with this id does not exist");
        }
        return storageUnit;
    }

    private void ensureStorageUnitExists(UUID storageUnitId) {
        if (storageUnitRepository.findById(new StorageUnitId(storageUnitId)).isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Storage unit with this id does not exist");
        }
    }

    public List<StorageUnit> getAllStorageUnits() {
        return (List<StorageUnit>) storageUnitRepository.findAll();
    }
}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain;

import jakarta.persistence.*;
import lombok.*;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.PhysicalAddress;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.valueObjects.Adress;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.valueObjects.StockLevel;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain.valueObjects.StorageUnitId;

import java.util.*;

@Entity
@Getter
@Setter
@AllArgsConstructor
@NoArgsConstructor
public class StorageUnit {

    @Setter(AccessLevel.PRIVATE)    // only for JPA
    @EmbeddedId
    private StorageUnitId id;

    private String name;

    private int fromZipCodeFirstDigit;

    private int toZipCodeFirstDigit;

    @Embedded
    private PhysicalAddress adress;

    @ElementCollection(fetch = FetchType.EAGER)
    private List<StockLevel> stockLevels;

    public StorageUnit(String name, PhysicalAddress adress, ArrayList<StockLevel> stockLevels) {
        validateStorageUnitName(name);
        validateStockLevels(stockLevels);

        this.id = new StorageUnitId();
        this.name = name;
        this.adress = adress;
        this.stockLevels = stockLevels;
    }

    public Set<ProductId> fulfillableShoppingCartParts(Map<ProductId, Integer> productQuantityMap) {
        Set<ProductId> fulfillableProducts = new HashSet<>();

        for (Map.Entry<ProductId, Integer> entry : productQuantityMap.entrySet()) {
            ProductId productId = entry.getKey();
            int requiredQuantity = entry.getValue();

            for (StockLevel stockLevel : this.stockLevels) {
                if (stockLevel.getProduct().getId().equals(productId) &&
                        stockLevel.getQuantityOfProducts() >= requiredQuantity) {
                    fulfillableProducts.add(productId);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }

        return fulfillableProducts;
    }

    private void validateStorageUnitName(String name) {
        if (name == null || name.trim().isEmpty()) {
            throw new ShopException("Name cannot be null or empty");
        }
    }


    private void validateStockLevels(List<StockLevel> stockLevels) {
        if (stockLevels == null) {
            throw new ShopException("Stock levels must not be null");
        }
    }


}


--- FILE: C:\workspace\Masterarbeit\Repositories\ST2M4_group_2767082b-b468-438e-b617-5205499d6937\src\main\java\thkoeln\archilab\ecommerce\solution\storageunit\domain\StorageUnitComparator.java ---
package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.storageunit.domain;

import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.domainprimitives.ZipCode;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.solution.product.domain.valueObjects.ProductId;

import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

public class StorageUnitComparator implements Comparator<StorageUnit> {
    private final Map<ProductId, Integer> shoppingCart;
    private final ZipCode userZip;

    public StorageUnitComparator(Map<ProductId, Integer> shoppingCart, ZipCode userZip) {
        this.shoppingCart = shoppingCart;
        this.userZip = userZip;
    }

    @Override
    public int compare(StorageUnit s1, StorageUnit s2) {
        Set<ProductId> s1Fulfillable = s1.fulfillableShoppingCartParts(shoppingCart);
        Set<ProductId> s2Fulfillable = s2.fulfillableShoppingCartParts(shoppingCart);

        int s1Count = s1Fulfillable.size();
        int s2Count = s2Fulfillable.size();

        if (s1Count != s2Count) {
            return Integer.compare(s2Count, s1Count); // Mehr erfüllte Produkte zuerst
        }

        // Bei Gleichstand: Nähe der Postleitzahl
        int s1ZipDiff = s1.getAdress().getZipCode().difference(userZip);
        int s2ZipDiff = s2.getAdress().getZipCode().difference(userZip);

        return Integer.compare(s1ZipDiff, s2ZipDiff); // Kleinere Entfernung zuerst
    }
}
