        expectedQuantityMap1.put( productId3, 3 );
        Map<UUID, Integer> quantityMap2 = new HashMap<>();
        quantityMap2.put( productId1, 1 );
        quantityMap2.put( productId3, 3 );

        // when
        // then
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId6, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId6, productId2, 2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId6, productId3, 3 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail6, expectedQuantityMap1 );

        shoppingCartRESTHelper.deleteProductFromShoppingCart( shoppingCartId6, productId2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail6, quantityMap2 );
    }

    }


    @Test
    public void testAddRemoveProductsFromAndToShoppingCart() throws Exception {
        // given
        UUID shoppingCartId3 = shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail3, emptyMap );
        UUID shoppingCartId5 = shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail6, emptyMap );

        // when
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId3, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId3, productId2, 3 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.deleteProductFromShoppingCart( shoppingCartId3, productId1 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId3, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId3, productId2, 6 );

        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId5, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId5, productId2, 8 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.deleteProductFromShoppingCart( shoppingCartId5, productId1 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId5, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId5, productId2, 2 );

        // then
        // user3 has 1x productId1 and 9x productId2 expected in cart
        Map<UUID, Integer> expectedMap3 = new HashMap<>();
        expectedMap3.put( productId1, 1 );
        expectedMap3.put( productId2, 9 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail3, expectedMap3 );

        // user6 has 1x productId1 and 10x productId2 in cart
        Map<UUID, Integer> expectedMap5 = new HashMap<>();
        expectedMap5.put( productId1, 1 );
        expectedMap5.put( productId2, 10 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail6, expectedMap5 );
    }


    @Test
    public void testNoDoubleCheckout() throws Exception {
        // given
        UUID shoppingCartId8 = shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart( userEmail8, emptyMap );

        // when
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId8, productId2, 3 );

        // then
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.checkout( shoppingCartId8, userName8, CREATED, null );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.checkout( shoppingCartId8, null, CONFLICT, null );
    }


    @Test
    public void testCheckout_1_Purchase() throws Exception {
        // given:
        // User 0 wants to buy 1x product 9. This is in storage unit 5, 7, and 8. Out of these,
        // storage unit 8 with zip code 89250 is closest to user 0 with zip code 02314.
        Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> expectedPurchases = new HashMap<>() {{
            put( storageUnitId8, map9_quantity_1 );
        }};
        UUID shoppingCartId0 = shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart(
                userEmail0, null );
        int stock9before =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId8, productId9 );

        // when
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId0, productId9, 1 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.checkout( shoppingCartId0, userName0, CREATED, expectedPurchases );
        int stock9after =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId8, productId9 );

        // then
        assertEquals( 1, stock9before - stock9after );
    }


    @Test
    public void testCheckout_3_Purchase() throws Exception {
        // given:
        // User 8 (Felix Bauer) wants to buy 2x each of products 5, 9, 11; and 7x product 7.
        //       - products 9 and 11 can both be found in storage units 7 and 8. Storage units 7 (76532) is closer to
        //         the user (70173)
        //       - product 7 is available in storage units 1, 2, and 3, but only storage unit 3 has enough stock.
        //       - product 5 is only available in storage unit 0.
        Map<UUID, Map<UUID, Integer>> expectedPurchases = new HashMap<>() {{
            put( storageUnitId0, map5_quantity_2 );
            put( storageUnitId3, map7_quantity_7 );
            put( storageUnitId7, map9_11_quantity_2_2 );
        }};
        UUID shoppingCartId8 = shoppingCartRESTHelper.getQueryShoppingCart(
                userEmail8, null );
        int stock5before =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );
        int stock7before =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId3, productId7 );
        int stock9before =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId7, productId9 );
        int stock11before =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId7, productId11 );

        // when
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId8, productId5, 2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId8, productId7, 7 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId8, productId9, 2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.addProductToShoppingCart( shoppingCartId8, productId11, 2 );
        shoppingCartRESTHelper.checkout( shoppingCartId8, userName8, CREATED, expectedPurchases );
        int stock5after =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );
        int stock7after =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId3, productId7 );
        int stock9after =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId7, productId9 );
        int stock11after =
                storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId7, productId11 );

        // then
        assertEquals( 2, stock5before - stock5after );
        assertEquals( 7, stock7before - stock7after );
        assertEquals( 2, stock9before - stock9after );
        assertEquals( 2, stock11before - stock11after );
    }


}

        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                        userEmail0, productId5, -1 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                        userEmail0, productId1, 4 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                        userEmail0, productId2, 5 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testAddRemoveProductsFromAndToShoppingCart() {
        // given
        UUID productId1 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 1 );
        UUID productId2 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 2 );
        EmailType userEmail3 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 3 );
        EmailType userEmail5 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 5 );

        // when user 3 ...
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail3, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail3, productId2, 3 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                userEmail3, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail3, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail3, productId2, 6 );
        Map<UUID, Integer> cart3 = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsMap( userEmail3 );
        // user3 has 1x productId1 and 9x productId2 in cart

        // ... and when user 5 ...
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail5, productId1, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail5, productId2, 8 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.removeProductFromShoppingCart(
                userEmail5, productId1, 1 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail5, productId2, 2 );
        Map<UUID, Integer> cart5 = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsMap( userEmail5 );
        // user5 has 1x productId1 and 10x productId2 in cart

        // then
        assertEquals( 2, cart3.size() );
        assertEquals( 1, cart3.get( productId1 ) );
        assertEquals( 9, cart3.get( productId2 ) );

        assertEquals( 2, cart5.size() );
        assertEquals( 1, cart5.get( productId1 ) );
        assertEquals( 10, cart5.get( productId2 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testShoppingCartValue() {
        // given
        UUID productId3 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 3 );
        UUID productId6 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 6 );
        UUID productId8 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 8 );
        MoneyType price3 = productTestHelper.getSalesPrice( 3 );
        MoneyType price6 = productTestHelper.getSalesPrice( 6 );
        MoneyType price8 = productTestHelper.getSalesPrice( 8 );
        EmailType userEmail3 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 3 );

        // when
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart( userEmail3, productId3, 3 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart( userEmail3, productId6, 2 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart( userEmail3, productId8, 5 );
        // user3 has 3x productId3, 2x productId6 and 5x productId8 in cart
        MoneyType cartValue = shoppingCartUseCases.getShoppingCartAsMoneyValue( userEmail3 );

        // then
        assertEquals( price3.multiplyBy( 3 ).add( price6.multiplyBy( 2 ) ).add( price8.multiplyBy( 5 ) ),
                cartValue );
    }

    @Test
    public void testUnsuccessfulCheckout() {
        // given user buying product 0 (which is not in stock), and user 1 buying product 1
        // in a bigger quantity (11) than available (10)
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        EmailType userEmail0 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 0 );
        EmailType userEmail1 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 1 );
        UUID productId0 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 0 );
        UUID productId1 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 1 );

        // when
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail0, productId0, 1 );
        shoppingCartUseCases.addProductToShoppingCart(
                userEmail1, productId1, 11 );

        // then
        assertThrows( InsufficientStockException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.checkout( userEmail0 ) );
        assertThrows( InsufficientStockException.class,
                () -> shoppingCartUseCases.checkout( userEmail1 ) );
    }

}

import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;

/**
 * This test checks the management and lifecycle of storage units.
 */
@SpringBootTest
public class StorageUnitManagementTest {

    private StorageUnitUseCases storageUnitUseCases;
    @Autowired
    private ProductCatalogUseCases productCatalogUseCases;
    @Autowired

    private UUID nonExistingId2;


    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() {
        purgatory.deleteEverything();
        productTestHelper.addAllProducts();

        somePhysicalAddress = instantiatePhysicalAddress( "Some Street", "Some City",
                instantiateZipCode( "90001" ) );
        nonExistingId1 = UUID.randomUUID();
        nonExistingId2 = UUID.randomUUID();
    }


    @Test
    public void testAddInvalidStorageUnit() {
        // given
        String name = "Lager1";

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.addNewStorageUnit(
                        null, somePhysicalAddress ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.addNewStorageUnit(
                        "", somePhysicalAddress ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.addNewStorageUnit(
                        name, null ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testDeleteAllStorageUnitsWhenEmpty() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( false );
        UUID productId9 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 9 );
        UUID storageUnitId1 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 1 );
        UUID storageUnitId2 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 2 );

        // when
        int numOf1 = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId1, productId9 );
        int numOf2 = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId2, productId9 );

        // then
        assertEquals( 0, numOf1 );
        assertEquals( 0, numOf2 );
        storageUnitUseCases.deleteAllStorageUnits();
        // ... ids must be invalid now
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId1, productId9 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId2, productId9 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testDeleteAllStorageUnitsWhenFull() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID productId7 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 7 );
        UUID storageUnitId1 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 1 );
        UUID storageUnitId2 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 2 );

        // when
        int numOf1 = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId1, productId7 );
        int numOf2 = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId2, productId7 );

        // then
        assertTrue( numOf1 == 3 );
        assertTrue( numOf2 == 3 );
        storageUnitUseCases.deleteAllStorageUnits();
        // ... ids must be invalid now
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId1, productId7 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId2, productId7 ) );
    }



    @Test
    public void testAddToStock() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in storage unit 0
        UUID storageUnitId0 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 0 );
        int originalStock5 =
                storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitStock( 0, 5 );

        // when
        int stock5before = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );
        storageUnitUseCases.addToStock( storageUnitId0, productId5, 23 );
        int stock5after = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );
        storageUnitUseCases.addToStock( storageUnitId0, productId5, 0 );
        int stock5after2 = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );

        // then
        assertEquals( originalStock5, stock5before );
        assertEquals( stock5before + 23, stock5after );
        assertEquals( stock5after, stock5after2 );
    }

    @Test
    public void testRemoveFromStock() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID storageUnitId0 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 0 );
        UUID productId0 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 0 ); // 0 in storage unit 0
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in storage unit 0
        UUID productId6 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 6 ); // random >30 in storage unit 0
        int stock0before =
                storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitStock( 0, 0 );
        int stock5before =
                storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitStock( 0, 5 );
        int stock6before =
                storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitStock( 0, 6 );

        // when
        storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock( storageUnitId0, productId5, 1 );
        int stock5after = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );
        storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock( storageUnitId0, productId0, 0 );
        int stock0after = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId0 );
        storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock(
                storageUnitId0, productId6, stock6before );
        int stock6after = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId6 );

        // then
        assertEquals( stock5before - 1, stock5after );
        assertEquals( stock0before, stock0after );
        assertEquals( 0, stock6after );
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidRemoveFromStock() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID storageUnitId0 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 0 );
        UUID productId0 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 0 ); // 0 in storage unit 0
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in storage unit 0
        int stock5before =
                storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitStock( 0, 5 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock( nonExistingId1, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock(
                        storageUnitId0, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock(
                        nonExistingId1, productId5, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock(
                        storageUnitId0, productId5, -1 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock(
                        storageUnitId0, productId5, stock5before + 1 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class,
                () -> storageUnitUseCases.removeFromStock(
                        storageUnitId0, productId0, 1 ) ); // already 0 in storage unit 0
    }


    @Test
    public void testChangeStock() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID storageUnitId0 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 0 );
        UUID productId5 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 5 ); // random >30 in storage unit 0

        // when
        storageUnitUseCases.changeStockTo( storageUnitId0, productId5, 111 );
        int stock5after = storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock( storageUnitId0, productId5 );

        // then
        assertEquals( 111, stock5after );
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidChangeStock() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID storageUnitId0 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 0 );
        UUID productId6 = productTestHelper.getProductId( 6 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> storageUnitUseCases.changeStockTo(
                nonExistingId1, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> storageUnitUseCases.changeStockTo(
                nonExistingId1, productId6, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> storageUnitUseCases.changeStockTo(
                storageUnitId0, nonExistingId2, 12 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> storageUnitUseCases.changeStockTo(
                storageUnitId0, productId6, -1 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testEmptyStorageUnit() {
        // given
        storageUnitTestHelper.addAllStorageUnits( true );
        UUID storageUnitId9 = storageUnitTestHelper.getStorageUnitId( 9 ); // empty storage unit

        // when
        int totalStock = 0;
        for ( int iProduct = 0; iProduct < productTestHelper.numberOfProducts(); iProduct++ ) {
            UUID productId = productTestHelper.getProductId( iProduct );
            totalStock += storageUnitUseCases.getAvailableStock(
                    storageUnitId9, productId );
        }

        // then
        assertEquals( 0, totalStock );
    }



}

            STORAGE_UNIT_DOMAIN_PACKAGE + ".StorageUnit";


    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() throws Exception {
        dpTestClass = new ClassFileImporter().importClass( DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest.class );
        restTestClass = new ClassFileImporter().importClass( OwnShoppingCartRESTTest.class );

        dpTestClasses = new ClassFileImporter().importClasses( DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest.class );
        restTestClasses = new ClassFileImporter().importClasses( OwnShoppingCartRESTTest.class );
    }


    @Test
    public void ensureMinimumNumberOfTestMethods() {
        // given
        // when
        int dpTestMethodCount = getTestMethodCount( dpTestClass );
        int restTestMethodCount = getTestMethodCount( restTestClass );

        // then
        assertTrue( "There should be at least 4 test methods in the dp test class, but there are only "
                        + dpTestMethodCount,dpTestMethodCount >= 2 );
        assertTrue( "There should be at least 5 test methods in the rest test class, but there are only "
                        + restTestMethodCount, restTestMethodCount >= 5 );
    }

    private int getTestMethodCount( JavaClass testClass ) {
        int testMethodCount = 0;
        for ( JavaMethod method : testClass.getMethods() ) {
            if ( isTestMethod( method ) ) {
                testMethodCount++;
            }
        }
        return testMethodCount;
    }

    private boolean isTestMethod( JavaMethod method ) {
        return method.isAnnotatedWith( Test.class );
    }


    @Test
    public void dpTestsShouldReferenceTheRightClasses() {
        ArchRule rule = classes()
                .should().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( ZipCodeType.class )
                .andShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( MoneyType.class )
                .andShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( PhysicalAddressType.class )
                .andShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( EmailType.class )
                .because( "DomainPrimitiveJSONSerializationTest should reference ZipCode, " +
                        "Money, Email, and PhysicalAddress!" );
        rule.check( dpTestClasses );
    }


    @Test
    public void restTestsShouldReferenceEmail() {
        ArchRule rule = classes()
                .should().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( EmailType.class )
                .because( "StorageUnitComparatorUnitTest should reference EmailType!" );
        rule.check( restTestClasses );
    }


    @Test
    public void restTestsShouldReferenceRESTControllers() {
        ArchRule rule = classes()
                .should().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAnnotatedWith( RestController.class )
                .orShould().dependOnClassesThat()
                .areAssignableTo( ShoppingCartRESTHelper.class )
                .because( "StorageUnitComparatorUnitTest should call REST controllers! " +
                        "(either directly or via the ShoppingCartRESTHelper REST helper)" );
        rule.check( restTestClasses );
    }

}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.user;

import org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.boot.test.context.SpringBootTest;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.ShopException;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.UserTestHelper;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.Purgatory;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserRegistrationUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PhysicalAddressType;

import static org.junit.jupiter.api.Assertions.*;
import static thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.FactoryMethodInvoker.*;


@SpringBootTest
public class UserRegistrationTest {
    @Autowired
    private UserRegistrationUseCases userRegistrationUseCases;
    @Autowired
    private Purgatory purgatory;
    @Autowired
    private UserTestHelper userTestHelper;

    private EmailType nonExistingEmail;
    private PhysicalAddressType somePhysicalAddress;

    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() {
        purgatory.deleteEverything();
        nonExistingEmail = instantiateEmail( "this@nononono.de" );
        somePhysicalAddress = instantiatePhysicalAddress( "Some Street", "Some City",
                instantiateZipCode( "90001" ) );
    }

    @Test
    public void testAllUsersRegistered() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();
        EmailType email3 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 3 );
        String name3 = userTestHelper.getUserName( 3 );
        PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress3 = userTestHelper.getUserPhysicalAddress( 3 );

        // when
        UserType user3 = userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData(
                email3 );

        // then
        Assertions.assertEquals( name3, user3.getName() );
        Assertions.assertEquals( email3, user3.getEmail() );
        Assertions.assertEquals( physicalAddress3, user3.getPhysicalAddress() );
    }


    @Test
    public void testRegisterUserWithDuplicateEmail() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();
        PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress5 = userTestHelper.getUserPhysicalAddress( 5 );
        EmailType email5 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 5 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.register( "Gandalf The Grey",
                        email5, physicalAddress5 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testRegisterUserWithDuplicateNameOrPhysicalAddress() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();
        EmailType newEmail =
                instantiateEmail( "some@this.de" );
        PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress2 = userTestHelper.getUserPhysicalAddress( 2 );
        String name2 = userTestHelper.getUserName( 2 );

        // when
        // then
        assertDoesNotThrow( () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.register( name2, newEmail, physicalAddress2 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testRegisterUserWithInvalidData() {
        // given
        EmailType email5 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 5 );
        PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress5 = userTestHelper.getUserPhysicalAddress( 5 );
        String name5 = userTestHelper.getUserName( 5 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.register( null, email5, physicalAddress5 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.register("", email5, physicalAddress5 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.register( name5, null, physicalAddress5 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.register( name5, email5, null ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testChangeAddressWithInvalidData() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();
        PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress7 = userTestHelper.getUserPhysicalAddress( 7 );
        EmailType email7 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 7 );

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.changeAddress( nonExistingEmail, physicalAddress7 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.changeAddress( null, physicalAddress7 ) );
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.changeAddress( email7, null ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testGetDataForNonexistingEmail() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData( nonExistingEmail ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testDeleteUsersNoMoreUsers() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();
        EmailType email0 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 0 );


        // when
        userRegistrationUseCases.deleteAllUsers();

        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () -> userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData(
                email0 ) );
    }


    @Test
    public void testChangeAddressSuccessful() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();
        EmailType email6 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 6 );

        // when
        userRegistrationUseCases.changeAddress( email6, somePhysicalAddress );
        UserType newUser6 =
                userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData( email6 );

        // then
        Assertions.assertEquals( email6, newUser6.getEmail() );
        Assertions.assertEquals( somePhysicalAddress, newUser6.getPhysicalAddress() );
    }


    @Test
    public void testChangeAddressForNonexistingEmail() {
        // given
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();

        // when
        // then
        assertThrows( ShopException.class, () ->
                userRegistrationUseCases.changeAddress( nonExistingEmail, somePhysicalAddress ) );
    }


}

package thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.tests.user;

import jakarta.transaction.Transactional;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.BeforeEach;
import org.junit.jupiter.api.Test;
import org.springframework.beans.factory.annotation.Autowired;
import org.springframework.boot.test.autoconfigure.web.servlet.AutoConfigureMockMvc;
import org.springframework.boot.test.context.SpringBootTest;
import org.springframework.context.annotation.Import;
import org.springframework.test.web.servlet.MockMvc;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.helpers.impl.RESTTestHelperConfiguration;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserRegistrationUseCases;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.UserType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.EmailType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.domainprimitivetypes.PhysicalAddressType;
import thkoeln.archilab.ecommerce.usecases.masterdata.*;

import java.util.UUID;

import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.request.MockMvcRequestBuilders.get;
import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.result.MockMvcResultMatchers.jsonPath;
import static org.springframework.test.web.servlet.result.MockMvcResultMatchers.status;

@SpringBootTest
@Transactional
@AutoConfigureMockMvc
@Import( RESTTestHelperConfiguration.class )
public class UserRESTTest {
    @Autowired
    private UserRegistrationUseCases userRegistrationUseCases;
    @Autowired
    private Purgatory purgatory;
    @Autowired
    private UserTestHelper userTestHelper;
    @Autowired
    private MockMvc mockMvc;

    private UUID randomId;
    private EmailType nonExistingEmail;

    @BeforeEach
    public void setUp() {
        purgatory.deleteEverything();
        userTestHelper.registerAllUsers();

        nonExistingEmail = FactoryMethodInvoker.instantiateEmail(
                "harry@sally.de" );
        randomId = UUID.randomUUID();
    }


    @Test
    public void testInvalidUserUris() throws Exception {
        // given
        String allUsersUri = "/users";
        String randomIdUri = "/users/" +  randomId;
        String nonExistingEmailUri = "/users?email=" + nonExistingEmail;
        String randomParamUri = "/users?randomParam=randomValue";

        // when
        // then
        mockMvc.perform( get( allUsersUri ) ).andExpect( status().isMethodNotAllowed() );
        mockMvc.perform( get( randomIdUri ) ).andExpect( status().isNotFound() );
        mockMvc.perform( get( nonExistingEmailUri ) ).andExpect( status().isNotFound() );
        mockMvc.perform( get( randomParamUri ) ).andExpect( status().is4xxClientError() );
    }


    @Test
    public void testRandomUserId() throws Exception {
        // given
        String invalidUri = "/users/" +  randomId;

        // when
        // then
        mockMvc.perform( get( invalidUri ) ).andExpect( status().isNotFound() );
    }


    @Test
    public void testQueryUser() throws Exception {
        // given
        EmailType email4 =
                userTestHelper.getUserEmail( 4 );
        String userUri4 = "/users?email=" + email4;

        // when
        UserType user4 = userRegistrationUseCases.getUserData( email4 );
        String name = userTestHelper.getUserName( 4 );
        PhysicalAddressType physicalAddress4 = userTestHelper.getUserPhysicalAddress( 4 );

        // then (check using JSONPath)
        mockMvc.perform( get( userUri4 ) )
                .andExpect( status().isOk() )
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$.name" ).value( name ) )
                // id is position 0 (cannot be tested with current API structure), name is position 1,
                // email is 2, physical address is 3)
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$..emailString" ).value( email4.toString() ) )
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$..city" ).value( physicalAddress4.getCity() ) )
                .andExpect( jsonPath( "$..zipCodeString" ).value(
                        physicalAddress4.getZipCode().toString() ) );
    }

}
